<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">1993 FIFA U-17 World Championship</h1>

<p>The <b>1993 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FIFA_U-17_World_Championship" title="FIFA U-17 World Championship">FIFA U-17 World Championship</a></b>, the fifth edition of the tournament, was held in the cities of <a href="/wiki/Tokyo" title="Tokyo">Tokyo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hiroshima" title="Hiroshima">Hiroshima</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kyoto" title="Kyoto">Kyoto</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kobe" title="Kobe">Kobe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nagoya" title="Nagoya">Nagoya</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gifu,_Gifu" title="Gifu, Gifu">Gifu City</a> in <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> between 21 August and 4 September 1993. Players born after 1 August 1976 were allowed to participate in the tournament.</p>
<p></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quarterfinals">Quarterfinals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993_FIFA_U-17_World_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Quarterfinals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="vevent" style="width: 100%; background-color: transparent; clear:both">
<p><span class="summary" style="display: none;"><a href="/wiki/Ghana_national_under-17_football_team" title="Ghana national under-17 football team">Ghana</a><span class="flagicon"> <img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="450" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Flag_of_Ghana.svg/23px-Flag_of_Ghana.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Flag_of_Ghana.svg/35px-Flag_of_Ghana.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Flag_of_Ghana.svg/45px-Flag_of_Ghana.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></span> v <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="640" data-file-width="1280" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/46px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Australia_national_under-17_soccer_team" title="Australia national under-17 soccer team">Australia</a></span></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Semifinals">Semifinals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993_FIFA_U-17_World_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Semifinals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="vevent" style="width: 100%; background-color: transparent; clear:both">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Result">Result</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993_FIFA_U-17_World_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Result">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable" style="text-align: center; margin: 0 auto;">
<tr>
<th> 1993 FIFA U-17 World Championship Winners </th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><b><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="800" height="23" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/45px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/68px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/90px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png 2x" width="45"/><br/>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Goalscorers">Goalscorers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993_FIFA_U-17_World_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Goalscorers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Wilson Oruma of Nigeria won the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_U-17_World_Cup#Awards" title="FIFA U-17 World Cup">Golden Shoe</a> award for scoring six goals. In total, 107 goals were scored by 56 different players, with only one of them credited as own goal.</p>
<dl>
<dt>6 goals</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria"><img alt="Nigeria" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="800" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/23px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/35px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/46px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Wilson_Oruma" title="Wilson Oruma">Wilson Oruma</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>

</dl>
